     <script type="text/javascript">
      $(function(){
 			var _wrap=$('.idx_mt .list ul');
 			var _interval=2000;
 			var _moving;
 			_wrap.hover(function(){
 				clearInterval(_moving);
 			},function(){
 				_moving=setInterval(function(){
 					var _field=_wrap.find('li:first');
 					var _=_field.height();
 					_field.animate({marginTop:-20+'px'},1000,function(){
 						_field.css('marginTop',0).appendTo(_wrap);
 					})
 				},_interval)
 			}).trigger('mouseleave');
 		});
     </script>

          $(function(){
 							$(".idx_adv_switch li:eq(0)").show();
 							$("#sc_prod dd").mouseover(function(){
 								var index = $("#sc_prod a").index($(this).children('a'));
 								$(".idx_adv_switch li").hide()
 								var adli = $(".idx_adv_switch li:eq("+index+")");
 								adli.show();
 								if(adli.children('a').size()) {
 									$(this).children('a').attr('href', adli.children('a').attr('href')).attr('target', '_blank')
 								}
 								return false;
 							});
 						});
         </script>

 							elem = $("#userpwd");
 							if(elem.val() == '') {
 								alert('请输入密码');
 								elem.focus();
 								return false;
 							}
 							var password = elem.val();
 							$.ajax({
 								type: 'POST',
 								url: '/member/user_ajax_login.php',
 								data:{
 									username:username,
 									password:password
 								},
 								success: function(data){
 									if(data.state==1) {
 										window.location.href="/member/";
 									} else {
 										alert(data.message);
 									}
 								},
 								dataType: 'json'
 							});
 						});
 					});
        </script>
        <div class="c">
        </div>

        </script>
       </td>
      </tr>

    <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
     /*	var sg1 = new ScrollPic();
 	sg1.scrollContId   = "pic_arr";
 	sg1.arrLeftId      = "sl";
 	sg1.arrRightId     = "sr";

 	var sg2 = new ScrollPic();
 	sg2.scrollContId   = "pic_arr2";
 	sg2.arrLeftId      = "sl2";
 	sg2.arrRightId     = "sr2";
 	sg2.frameWidth     = 533;
 	sg2.pageWidth      = 113;
 	sg2.speed          = 10;
 	sg2.space          = 10;
 	sg2.autoPlay       = true;
 	sg2.autoPlayTime   = 3;
 	sg2.initialize();
 
 	var sg3 = new ScrollPic();
 	sg3.scrollContId   = "pic_arr3";
 	sg3.arrLeftId      = "sl3";
 	sg3.arrRightId     = "sr3";
 	sg3.frameWidth     = 533;
 	sg3.pageWidth      = 113;
 	sg3.speed          = 10;
 	sg3.space          = 10;
 	sg3.autoPlay       = true;
 	sg3.autoPlayTime   = 3;
 	sg3.initialize();	
 
 	$(function(){
 		$("[id=scpic]").each(function(){
 			var flag = 1;
 			var maxpic = $(this).find(".maxpic")
 			$(this).find('ul img').mouseenter(function(){
 				maxpic.html('<img src="'+$(this).attr('src')+'" alt="" width="100%" height="100%"/>').show();
 				flag = 1;
 			}).mouseleave(function(){
 				flag = 0
 				setTimeout(function(){
 					if(flag == 0) {
 						maxpic.hide();
 					}
 				},200);
 			});
 			maxpic.mouseenter(function(){
 				flag = 1
 			}).mouseleave(function(){
 				flag = 0
 				setTimeout(function(){
 					if(flag == 0) {
 						maxpic.hide();
 					}
 				},200);
 			});
 		});
 
 		$(".idx_area td").hover(function(){
 			$(this).addClass('on');
 			$(this).find(".td_blue").show();
                             
 		},function(){
 			$(this).removeClass('on');
 			$(this).find(".td_blue").hide();
 		})
 		setInterval('auto_scroll_vertical(".ids_p")',5000);
 	});
 
 	function auto_scroll_vertical(obj){
 		$(obj).find("div.sg_div").animate({
 			marginTop : "-174px"
 		},700,function(){
 			$(this).css({
 				marginTop : "0px"
 			}).find("ul:first").appendTo(this);
 			var prevElem = $(obj).prev();
 			var nextElem = prevElem.find('.on').next();
 			prevElem.children().removeClass('on');
 			if(nextElem.size()) {
 				nextElem.addClass('on');
 			} else {
 				prevElem.children(":eq(0)").addClass('on');
 			}
 		})
 	}
 
 	function scroll_news(id){
 		$(document).ready(function(){
 			$('#'+id+' li').eq(0).fadeOut('slow',function(){
 				$(this).clone().appendTo($(this).parent()).fadeIn('slow');
 				$(this).remove();
 			})
 		})
 	}
 	setInterval("scroll_news('rolltext')",3000);
 	setInterval("scroll_news('rolltext1')",3000);
 	setInterval("scroll_news('rolltext2')",3000);
 	setInterval("scroll_news('rolltext3')",3000);
 	setInterval("scroll_news('rolltext4')",3000);
 	setInterval("scroll_news('rolltext5')",3000);
 	
 	function auto_scroll_vertical2(obj){
 		$(obj).find("ul").animate({
 			marginTop : "-24px"
 		},400,function(){
 			$(this).css({
 				marginTop : "0px"
 			}).find("li:first").appendTo($(this));
 		})
 	}
 	$(function(){ 
 		setInterval('auto_scroll_vertical2("#microbus")',2500);
 	})
    </script>
